### 3. **ç»„ä»¶é—´è·å¯è§†åŒ–å·¥å…·**

```javascript:/Users/huijoohwee/Documents/GitHub/299_project-test/PRJT0001_MAPSXPLR_202507201916-v0.0.1/src/utils/spacingVisualizer.js
export class SpacingVisualizer {
  constructor() {
    this.isActive = false;
    this.overlays = [];
  }

  toggle() {
    if (this.isActive) {
      this.hide();
    } else {
      this.show();
    }
  }

  show() {
    this.isActive = true;
    this.createOverlays();
  }

  hide() {
    this.isActive = false;
    this.overlays.forEach(overlay => overlay.remove());
    this.overlays = [];
  }

  createOverlays() {
    const elements = document.querySelectorAll('*');
    
    elements.forEach(el => {
      const computed = getComputedStyle(el);
      const rect = el.getBoundingClientRect();
      
      // è·³è¿‡å¤ªå°çš„å…ƒç´ 
      if (rect.width < 10 || rect.height < 10) return;
      
      const padding = {
        top: parseInt(computed.paddingTop),
        right: parseInt(computed.paddingRight),
        bottom: parseInt(computed.paddingBottom),
        left: parseInt(computed.paddingLeft)
      };
      
      const margin = {
        top: parseInt(computed.marginTop),
        right: parseInt(computed.marginRight),
        bottom: parseInt(computed.marginBottom),
        left: parseInt(computed.marginLeft)
      };
      
      // åˆ›å»ºpaddingè¦†ç›–å±‚
      if (padding.top || padding.right || padding.bottom || padding.left) {
        this.createPaddingOverlay(rect, padding);
      }
      
      // åˆ›å»ºmarginè¦†ç›–å±‚
      if (margin.top || margin.right || margin.bottom || margin.left) {
        this.createMarginOverlay(rect, margin);
      }
    });
  }

  createPaddingOverlay(rect, padding) {
    const overlay = document.createElement('div');
    overlay.className = 'spacing-overlay padding-overlay';
    overlay.style.cssText = `
      position: fixed;
      pointer-events: none;
      z-index: 9997;
      background: rgba(0, 255, 0, 0.2);
      border: 1px solid rgba(0, 255, 0, 0.5);
      left: ${rect.left + window.scrollX}px;
      top: ${rect.top + window.scrollY}px;
      width: ${rect.width}px;
      height: ${rect.height}px;
    `;
    
    // æ·»åŠ æ ‡ç­¾
    const label = document.createElement('div');
    label.textContent = `P: ${padding.top}/${padding.right}/${padding.bottom}/${padding.left}`;
    label.style.cssText = `
      position: absolute;
      top: -20px;
      left: 0;
      background: rgba(0, 255, 0, 0.8);
      color: white;
      padding: 2px 6px;
      font-size: 10px;
      border-radius: 3px;
    `;
    
    overlay.appendChild(label);
    document.body.appendChild(overlay);
    this.overlays.push(overlay);
  }

  createMarginOverlay(rect, margin) {
    const overlay = document.createElement('div');
    overlay.className = 'spacing-overlay margin-overlay';
    overlay.style.cssText = `
      position: fixed;
      pointer-events: none;
      z-index: 9996;
      background: rgba(255, 165, 0, 0.2);
      border: 1px solid rgba(255, 165, 0, 0.5);
      left: ${rect.left + window.scrollX - margin.left}px;
      top: ${rect.top + window.scrollY - margin.top}px;
      width: ${rect.width + margin.left + margin.right}px;
      height: ${rect.height + margin.top + margin.bottom}px;
    `;
    
    // æ·»åŠ æ ‡ç­¾
    const label = document.createElement('div');
    label.textContent = `M: ${margin.top}/${margin.right}/${margin.bottom}/${margin.left}`;
    label.style.cssText = `
      position: absolute;
      top: -20px;
      right: 0;
      background: rgba(255, 165, 0, 0.8);
      color: white;
      padding: 2px 6px;
      font-size: 10px;
      border-radius: 3px;
    `;
    
    overlay.appendChild(label);
    document.body.appendChild(overlay);
    this.overlays.push(overlay);
  }
}

// å…¨å±€è®¿é—®
if (import.meta.env.DEV) {
  window.spacingVisualizer = new SpacingVisualizer();
}
```

### 4. **æ€§èƒ½ç›‘æ§é¢æ¿**

```vue:/Users/huijoohwee/Documents/GitHub/299_project-test/PRJT0001_MAPSXPLR_202507201916-v0.0.1/src/components/UI/PerformanceMonitor.vue
<template>
  <div v-if="isDev && isVisible" class="performance-monitor">
    <div class="monitor-header">
      <h4>âš¡ æ€§èƒ½ç›‘æ§</h4>
      <button @click="isVisible = false">Ã—</button>
    </div>
    
    <div class="metrics">
      <div class="metric">
        <span class="label">FPS:</span>
        <span class="value" :class="{ warning: fps < 30, error: fps < 15 }">
          {{ fps.toFixed(1) }}
        </span>
      </div>
      
      <div class="metric">
        <span class="label">å†…å­˜:</span>
        <span class="value">{{ memoryUsage }}MB</span>
      </div>
      
      <div class="metric">
        <span class="label">DOMèŠ‚ç‚¹:</span>
        <span class="value">{{ domNodes }}</span>
      </div>
      
      <div class="metric">
        <span class="label">æ¸²æŸ“æ—¶é—´:</span>
        <span class="value">{{ renderTime.toFixed(2) }}ms</span>
      </div>
    </div>
    
    <div class="chart">
      <canvas ref="chartCanvas" width="200" height="60"></canvas>
    </div>
  </div>
</template>

<script setup lang="ts">
import { ref, onMounted, onUnmounted } from 'vue'

const isDev = import.meta.env.DEV
const isVisible = ref(true)
const fps = ref(60)
const memoryUsage = ref(0)
const domNodes = ref(0)
const renderTime = ref(0)
const chartCanvas = ref<HTMLCanvasElement>()

let animationId: number
let lastTime = 0
let frameCount = 0
let fpsHistory: number[] = []

const updateMetrics = (currentTime: number) => {
  frameCount++
  
  if (currentTime - lastTime >= 1000) {
    fps.value = frameCount
    frameCount = 0
    lastTime = currentTime
    
    // æ›´æ–°å…¶ä»–æŒ‡æ ‡
    updateMemoryUsage()
    updateDOMNodes()
    updateRenderTime()
    
    // æ›´æ–°å›¾è¡¨
    updateChart()
  }
  
  animationId = requestAnimationFrame(updateMetrics)
}

const updateMemoryUsage = () => {
  if ('memory' in performance) {
    const memory = (performance as any).memory
    memoryUsage.value = Math.round(memory.usedJSHeapSize / 1024 / 1024)
  }
}

const updateDOMNodes = () => {
  domNodes.value = document.querySelectorAll('*').length
}

const updateRenderTime = () => {
  const start = performance.now()
  requestAnimationFrame(() => {
    renderTime.value = performance.now() - start
  })
}

const updateChart = () => {
  if (!chartCanvas.value) return
  
  fpsHistory.push(fps.value)
  if (fpsHistory.length > 50) {
    fpsHistory.shift()
  }
  
  const ctx = chartCanvas.value.getContext('2d')
  if (!ctx) return
  
  ctx.clearRect(0, 0, 200, 60)
  
  // ç»˜åˆ¶FPSæ›²çº¿
  ctx.strokeStyle = fps.value >= 30 ? '#10b981' : fps.value >= 15 ? '#f59e0b' : '#ef4444'
  ctx.lineWidth = 2
  ctx.beginPath()
  
  fpsHistory.forEach((value, index) => {
    const x = (index / (fpsHistory.length - 1)) * 200
    const y = 60 - (value / 60) * 60
    
    if (index === 0) {
      ctx.moveTo(x, y)
    } else {
      ctx.lineTo(x, y)
    }
  })
  
  ctx.stroke()
  
  // ç»˜åˆ¶åŸºå‡†çº¿
  ctx.strokeStyle = 'rgba(255, 255, 255, 0.3)'
  ctx.lineWidth = 1
  ctx.setLineDash([2, 2])
  
  // 60 FPSçº¿
  ctx.beginPath()
  ctx.moveTo(0, 0)
  ctx.lineTo(200, 0)
  ctx.stroke()
  
  // 30 FPSçº¿
  ctx.beginPath()
  ctx.moveTo(0, 30)
  ctx.lineTo(200, 30)
  ctx.stroke()
  
  ctx.setLineDash([])
}

onMounted(() => {
  if (isDev) {
    animationId = requestAnimationFrame(updateMetrics)
  }
})

onUnmounted(() => {
  if (animationId) {
    cancelAnimationFrame(animationId)
  }
})
</script>

<style scoped>
.performance-monitor {
  position: fixed;
  top: 20px;
  left: 20px;
  background: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.9);
  color: white;
  padding: 15px;
  border-radius: 8px;
  z-index: 9999;
  font-size: 12px;
  min-width: 220px;
  backdrop-filter: blur(10px);
}

.monitor-header {
  display: flex;
  justify-content: space-between;
  align-items: center;
  margin-bottom: 10px;
}

.monitor-header button {
  background: none;
  border: none;
  color: white;
  cursor: pointer;
  font-size: 16px;
}

.metrics {
  margin-bottom: 10px;
}

.metric {
  display: flex;
  justify-content: space-between;
  margin-bottom: 5px;
}

.value {
  font-weight: bold;
}

.value.warning {
  color: #f59e0b;
}

.value.error {
  color: #ef4444;
}

.chart {
  border: 1px solid rgba(255, 255, 255, 0.2);
  border-radius: 4px;
}
</style>
```

### 5. **å¿«é€ŸåŸå‹å·¥å…·**

```javascript:/Users/huijoohwee/Documents/GitHub/299_project-test/PRJT0001_MAPSXPLR_202507201916-v0.0.1/src/utils/prototypeTools.js
export class PrototypeTools {
  constructor() {
    this.init();
  }

  init() {
    if (!import.meta.env.DEV) return;
    
    this.addQuickActions();
    this.addComponentLibrary();
  }

  addQuickActions() {
    const toolbar = document.createElement('div');
    toolbar.id = 'prototype-toolbar';
    toolbar.innerHTML = `
      <div class="toolbar">
        <button onclick="prototypeTools.addTimelineItem()">+ æ—¶é—´çº¿é¡¹</button>
        <button onclick="prototypeTools.addLocationCard()">+ ä½ç½®å¡ç‰‡</button>
        <button onclick="prototypeTools.toggleDarkMode()">ğŸŒ™ æ·±è‰²æ¨¡å¼</button>
        <button onclick="prototypeTools.randomizeColors()">ğŸ¨ éšæœºé…è‰²</button>
        <button onclick="prototypeTools.exportPrototype()">ğŸ“¤ å¯¼å‡ºåŸå‹</button>
      </div>
    `;
    
    const style = document.createElement('style');
    style.textContent = `
      .toolbar {
        position: fixed;
        bottom: 20px;
        right: 20px;
        display: flex;
        gap: 8px;
        background: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.9);
        padding: 10px;
        border-radius: 8px;
        z-index: 9999;
      }
      .toolbar button {
        padding: 8px 12px;
        background: #3b82f6;
        color: white;
        border: none;
        border-radius: 4px;
        cursor: pointer;
        font-size: 12px;
      }
      .toolbar button:hover {
        background: #2563eb;
      }
    `;
    
    document.head.appendChild(style);
    document.body.appendChild(toolbar);
    
    window.prototypeTools = this;
  }

  addTimelineItem() {
    const container = document.getElementById('timeline-container');
    if (!container) return;
    
    const item = document.createElement('div');
    item.className = 'timeline-item fade-in';
    item.innerHTML = `
      <div class="timeline-time">æ–°æ—¶é—´</div>
      <div class="timeline-connector">
        <div class="timeline-dot"></div>
        <div class="timeline-line"></div>
      </div>
      <div class="timeline-content">
        <div class="timeline-title">æ–°åœ°ç‚¹</div>
        <div class="timeline-description">ç‚¹å‡»ç¼–è¾‘æè¿°</div>
        <div class="timeline-duration">â±ï¸ 1å°æ—¶</div>
      </div>
    `;
    
    container.appendChild(item);
    this.makeEditable(item);
  }

  addLocationCard() {
    const container = document.querySelector('.location-list') || document.body;
    
    const card = document.createElement('div');
    card.className = 'location-card fade-in';
    card.innerHTML = `
      <div class="card-time-badge">æ–°æ—¶é—´</div>
      <div class="card-sequence-badge">?</div>
      <h3>æ–°ä½ç½®</h3>
      <p>ç‚¹å‡»ç¼–è¾‘æè¿°</p>
    `;
    
    container.appendChild(card);
    this.makeEditable(card);
  }

  makeEditable(element) {
    const editableElements = element.querySelectorAll('.timeline-title, .timeline-description, h3, p');
    
    editableElements.forEach(el => {
      el.contentEditable = 'true';
      el.style.outline = 'none';
      
      el.addEventListener('focus', () => {
        el.style.background = 'rgba(59, 130, 246, 0.1)';
      });
      
      el.addEventListener('blur', () => {
        el.style.background = '';
      });
    });
  }

  toggleDarkMode() {
    document.body.classList.toggle('light-mode');
    
    if (document.body.classList.contains('light-mode')) {
      document.body.style.background = '#f9fafb';
      document.body.style.color = '#111827';
    } else {
      document.body.style.background = '#1f2937';
      document.body.style.color = '#ffffff';
    }
  }

  randomizeColors() {
    const colors = [
      '#ef4444', '#f97316', '#f59e0b', '#eab308',
      '#84cc16', '#22c55e', '#10b981', '#14b8a6',
      '#06b6d4', '#0ea5e9', '#3b82f6', '#6366f1',
      '#8b5cf6', '#a855f7', '#d946ef', '#ec4899'
    ];
    
    const elements = document.querySelectorAll('.timeline-dot, .card-time-badge, .timeline-time');
    
    elements.forEach(el => {
      const randomColor = colors[Math.floor(Math.random() * colors.length)];
      el.style.backgroundColor = randomColor;
    });
  }

  exportPrototype() {
    const html = document.documentElement.outerHTML;
    const blob = new Blob([html], { type: 'text/html' });
    const url = URL.createObjectURL(blob);
    
    const a = document.createElement('a');
    a.href = url;
    a.download = `prototype-${new Date().toISOString().slice(0, 10)}.html`;
    a.click();
    
    URL.revokeObjectURL(url);
  }
}

// è‡ªåŠ¨åˆå§‹åŒ–
if (import.meta.env.DEV) {
  new PrototypeTools();
}
```

```astro:/Users/huijoohwee/Documents/GitHub/src/pages/admin.astro
      data() {
        return {
          systemStatus: {
            healthy: true,
            message: 'ç³»ç»Ÿè¿è¡Œæ­£å¸¸',
            color: 'text-green-500'
          },
          lastBackup: {
            time: '2å°æ—¶å‰',
            type: 'å¢é‡å¤‡ä»½'

          performance: {
            avgResponseTime: 245

          errorStats: {

          recentLogs: [

          backupLoading: false,
          cacheLoading: false,
          securityLoading: false,
          optimizeLoading: false

      methods: {
        async triggerBackup() {
          this.backupLoading = true
          try {
            // æ¨¡æ‹ŸAPIè°ƒç”¨
            await new Promise(resolve => setTimeout(resolve, 2000))
            this.$message.success('å¤‡ä»½ä»»åŠ¡å·²å¯åŠ¨')

            this.$message.error('å¤‡ä»½å¯åŠ¨å¤±è´¥')
          } finally {
            this.backupLoading = false
          }
        },
        async clearCache() {
          this.cacheLoading = true
          try {
            await new Promise(resolve => setTimeout(resolve, 1000))
            this.$message.success('ç¼“å­˜æ¸…ç†å®Œæˆ')
          } catch (error) {
            this.$message.error('ç¼“å­˜æ¸…ç†å¤±è´¥')
          } finally {
            this.cacheLoading = false
          }
        },
        async runSecurityCheck() {
          this.securityLoading = true
          try {
            await new Promise(resolve => setTimeout(resolve, 3000))
            this.$message.success('å®‰å…¨æ£€æŸ¥å·²å®Œæˆ')
          } catch (error) {
            this.$message.error('å®‰å…¨æ£€æŸ¥å¤±è´¥')
          } finally {
            this.securityLoading = false
          }
        },
        async optimizePerformance() {
          this.optimizeLoading = true
          try {
            await new Promise(resolve => setTimeout(resolve, 2500))
            this.$message.success('æ€§èƒ½ä¼˜åŒ–å®Œæˆ')
          } catch (error) {
            this.$message.error('æ€§èƒ½ä¼˜åŒ–å¤±è´¥')
          } finally {
            this.optimizeLoading = false
          }
        },
        formatTime(timestamp) {
          return new Date(timestamp).toLocaleTimeString()
        }
      },
      mounted() {
        // å®šæ—¶åˆ·æ–°ç³»ç»ŸçŠ¶æ€
        setInterval(() => {
          // æ¨¡æ‹ŸçŠ¶æ€æ›´æ–°
          this.performance.avgResponseTime = Math.floor(Math.random() * 100) + 200
        }, 30000)
      }
    }

    // åˆ›å»ºåº”ç”¨å®ä¾‹
    const app = createApp(SystemDashboard)
    app.use(ElementPlus)
    app.mount('#admin-dashboard')
```

```astro:/Users/huijoohwee/Documents/GitHub/src/pages/admin.astro
                    <h3>24hé”™è¯¯</h3>
                    <p>{{ errorStats.count }}</p>
                  </div>
                </div>
              </el-card>
            </el-col>
          </el-row>
          
          <!-- æ“ä½œé¢æ¿ -->
          <el-row :gutter="20" class="mt-6">
            <el-col :span="12">
              <el-card>
                <template #header>
                  <h3>ç³»ç»Ÿæ“ä½œ</h3>
                </template>
                
                <div class="action-buttons">
                  <el-button type="primary" @click="triggerBackup" :loading="backupLoading">
                    <el-icon><FolderAdd /></el-icon>
                    ç«‹å³å¤‡ä»½
                  </el-button>
                  
                  <el-button type="warning" @click="clearCache" :loading="cacheLoading">
                    <el-icon><Delete /></el-icon>
                    æ¸…ç†ç¼“å­˜
                  </el-button>
                  
                  <el-button type="info" @click="runSecurityCheck" :loading="securityLoading">
                    <el-icon><Lock /></el-icon>
                    å®‰å…¨æ£€æŸ¥
                  </el-button>
                  
                  <el-button type="success" @click="optimizePerformance" :loading="optimizeLoading">
                    <el-icon><Promotion /></el-icon>
                    æ€§èƒ½ä¼˜åŒ–
                  </el-button>
                </div>
              </el-card>
            </el-col>

              <el-card>
                <template #header>
                  <h3>ç³»ç»Ÿæ—¥å¿—</h3>
                </template>
                
                <div class="log-container">
                  <div v-for="log in recentLogs" :key="log.id" class="log-entry" :class="log.level">
                    <span class="log-time">{{ formatTime(log.timestamp) }}</span>
                    <span class="log-level">{{ log.level }}</span>
                    <span class="log-message">{{ log.message }}</span>
                  </div>
                </div>
              </el-card>
            </el-col>
          </el-row>
        </div>
      `,
      data() {
        return {
          systemStatus: {
            healthy: true,
            message: 'ç³»ç»Ÿè¿è¡Œæ­£å¸¸',
            color: 'text-green-500'
          },
          lastBackup: {
            time: '2å°æ—¶å‰',
            type: 'å¢é‡å¤‡ä»½'
          },
          performance: {
            avgResponseTime: 245
          },
          errorStats: {
            count: 3
          },
          recentLogs: [
            { id: 1, timestamp: Date.now(), level: 'INFO', message: 'ç³»ç»Ÿå¯åŠ¨å®Œæˆ' },
            { id: 2, timestamp: Date.now() - 60000, level: 'WARN', message: 'APIå“åº”æ—¶é—´è¾ƒæ…¢' },
            { id: 3, timestamp: Date.now() - 120000, level: 'ERROR', message: 'å¤‡ä»½ä»»åŠ¡å¤±è´¥' }
          ],
          backupLoading: false,
          cacheLoading: false,
          securityLoading: false,
          optimizeLoading: false
        }
      },
      methods: {
        async triggerBackup() {
          this.backupLoading = true
          try {
            // æ¨¡æ‹ŸAPIè°ƒç”¨
            await new Promise(resolve => setTimeout(resolve, 2000))
            this.$message.success('å¤‡ä»½ä»»åŠ¡å·²å¯åŠ¨')
          } catch (error) {
            this.$message.error('å¤‡ä»½å¯åŠ¨å¤±è´¥')
          } finally {
            this.backupLoading = false
          }
        },
        async clearCache() {
          this.cacheLoading = true
          try {
            await new Promise(resolve => setTimeout(resolve, 1000))
            this.$message.success('ç¼“å­˜æ¸…ç†å®Œæˆ')
          } catch (error) {
            this.$message.error('ç¼“å­˜æ¸…ç†å¤±è´¥')
          } finally {
            this.cacheLoading = false
          }
        },
        async runSecurityCheck() {
          this.securityLoading = true
          try {
            await new Promise(resolve => setTimeout(resolve, 3000))
            this.$message.success('å®‰å…¨æ£€æŸ¥å·²å®Œæˆ')
          } catch (error) {
            this.$message.error('å®‰å…¨æ£€æŸ¥å¤±è´¥')
          } finally {
            this.securityLoading = false
          }
        },
        async optimizePerformance() {
          this.optimizeLoading = true
          try {
            await new Promise(resolve => setTimeout(resolve, 2500))
            this.$message.success('æ€§èƒ½ä¼˜åŒ–å®Œæˆ')
          } catch (error) {
            this.$message.error('æ€§èƒ½ä¼˜åŒ–å¤±è´¥')
          } finally {
            this.optimizeLoading = false
          }
        },
        formatTime(timestamp) {
          return new Date(timestamp).toLocaleTimeString()
        }
      },
      mounted() {
        // å®šæ—¶åˆ·æ–°ç³»ç»ŸçŠ¶æ€
        setInterval(() => {
          // æ¨¡æ‹ŸçŠ¶æ€æ›´æ–°
          this.performance.avgResponseTime = Math.floor(Math.random() * 100) + 200
        }, 30000)
      }
    }

    // åˆ›å»ºåº”ç”¨å®ä¾‹
    const app = createApp(SystemDashboard)
    app.use(ElementPlus)
    app.mount('#admin-dashboard')
  })
</script>
```

## 1. åˆ›å»ºç¼ºå¤±çš„ locationStore

```typescript:/Users/huijoohwee/Documents/GitHub/299_project-test/PRJT0001_MAPSXPLR_202507201916-v0.0.1/src/stores/locationStore.ts
import { defineStore } from 'pinia'
import { ref, computed } from 'vue'

export interface Location {
  id: number
  name: string
  coordinates: [number, number]
  description?: string
  timestamp: string
  category?: string
  rating?: number
}

export interface TimelineItem {
  time: string
  title: string
  description: string
  duration: string
  locationId?: number
}

export const useLocationStore = defineStore('location', () => {
  // çŠ¶æ€
  const locations = ref<Location[]>([])
  const timelineItems = ref<TimelineItem[]>([])
  const currentLocation = ref<Location | null>(null)
  const selectedLocation = ref<Location | null>(null)

  // è®¡ç®—å±æ€§
  const locationCount = computed(() => locations.value.length)
  const hasLocations = computed(() => locations.value.length > 0)

  // æ–¹æ³•
  const addLocation = (location: Omit<Location, 'id' | 'timestamp'>) => {
    const newLocation: Location = {
      ...location,
      id: Date.now(),
      timestamp: new Date().toISOString()
    }
    locations.value.push(newLocation)
    return newLocation
  }

  const removeLocation = (id: number) => {
    const index = locations.value.findIndex(loc => loc.id === id)
    if (index > -1) {
      locations.value.splice(index, 1)
      return true
    }
    return false
  }

  const updateLocation = (id: number, updates: Partial<Location>) => {
    const location = locations.value.find(loc => loc.id === id)
    if (location) {
      Object.assign(location, updates)
      return location
    }
    return null
  }

  const getLocationById = (id: number) => {
    return locations.value.find(loc => loc.id === id)
  }

  const setCurrentLocation = (location: Location | null) => {
    currentLocation.value = location
  }

  const setSelectedLocation = (location: Location | null) => {
    selectedLocation.value = location
  }

  // Timeline ç›¸å…³æ–¹æ³•
  const addTimelineItem = (item: TimelineItem) => {
    timelineItems.value.push(item)
  }

  const removeTimelineItem = (index: number) => {
    if (index >= 0 && index < timelineItems.value.length) {
      timelineItems.value.splice(index, 1)
    }
  }

  const updateTimelineItem = (index: number, updates: Partial<TimelineItem>) => {
    if (index >= 0 && index < timelineItems.value.length) {
      Object.assign(timelineItems.value[index], updates)
    }
  }

  const clearTimeline = () => {
    timelineItems.value = []
  }

  const generateTimelineFromLocations = () => {
    const items: TimelineItem[] = locations.value.map((location, index) => ({
      time: `${9 + index * 2}:00`,
      title: location.name,
      description: location.description || 'æ¢ç´¢è¿™ä¸ªç²¾å½©çš„åœ°ç‚¹',
      duration: '2å°æ—¶',
      locationId: location.id
    }))
    timelineItems.value = items
  }

  // åˆå§‹åŒ–æ¨¡æ‹Ÿæ•°æ®
  const initializeMockData = () => {
    const mockLocations: Omit<Location, 'id' | 'timestamp'>[] = [
      {
        name: 'å¤©å®‰é—¨å¹¿åœº',
        coordinates: [116.3974, 39.9093],
        description: 'ä¸­å›½çš„è±¡å¾æ€§åœ°æ ‡',
        category: 'å†å²æ™¯ç‚¹',
        rating: 5
      },
      {
        name: 'æ•…å®«åšç‰©é™¢',
        coordinates: [116.3972, 39.9180],
        description: 'æ˜æ¸…ä¸¤ä»£çš„çš‡å®¶å®«æ®¿',
        category: 'å†å²æ™¯ç‚¹',
        rating: 5
      },
      {
        name: 'é¢å’Œå›­',
        coordinates: [116.2732, 39.9990],
        description: 'æ¸…ä»£çš‡å®¶å›­æ—',
        category: 'å›­æ—æ™¯ç‚¹',
        rating: 4
      }
    ]

    mockLocations.forEach(loc => addLocation(loc))
    generateTimelineFromLocations()
  }

  return {
    // çŠ¶æ€
    locations,
    timelineItems,
    currentLocation,
    selectedLocation,
    
    // è®¡ç®—å±æ€§
    locationCount,
    hasLocations,
    
    // æ–¹æ³•
    addLocation,
    removeLocation,
    updateLocation,
    getLocationById,
    setCurrentLocation,
    setSelectedLocation,
    
    // Timeline æ–¹æ³•
    addTimelineItem,
    removeTimelineItem,
    updateTimelineItem,
    clearTimeline,
    generateTimelineFromLocations,
    initializeMockData
  }
})
```

```astro:/Users/huijoohwee/Documents/GitHub/299_project-test/PRJT0001_MAPSXPLR_202507201916-v0.0.1/src/pages/admin.astro
  <!-- Vue 3 -->

  <script>
    const { createApp, ref, onMounted } = Vue;
    
    createApp({
      setup() {
        const systemStats = ref({
          activeUsers: 0,
          totalLocations: 0,
          systemUptime: '0h',
          memoryUsage: 0
        });
        
        const recentLogs = ref([]);
        
        const loadSystemStats = async () => {
          // æ¨¡æ‹Ÿæ•°æ®åŠ è½½
          systemStats.value = {
            activeUsers: Math.floor(Math.random() * 100) + 50,
            totalLocations: Math.floor(Math.random() * 500) + 200,
            systemUptime: `${Math.floor(Math.random() * 24)}h ${Math.floor(Math.random() * 60)}m`,
            memoryUsage: Math.floor(Math.random() * 30) + 40
          };
        };
        
        const loadRecentLogs = () => {
          const logLevels = ['INFO', 'WARN', 'ERROR', 'DEBUG'];
          const messages = [
            'ç”¨æˆ·ç™»å½•æˆåŠŸ',
            'åœ°å›¾æ•°æ®æ›´æ–°å®Œæˆ',
            'ç¼“å­˜æ¸…ç†å®Œæˆ',
            'å¤‡ä»½ä»»åŠ¡æ‰§è¡Œ',
            'æ€§èƒ½ç›‘æ§æŠ¥å‘Šç”Ÿæˆ',
            'å®‰å…¨æ£€æŸ¥é€šè¿‡'
          ];
          
          recentLogs.value = Array.from({ length: 10 }, (_, i) => ({
            id: i,
            timestamp: new Date(Date.now() - i * 60000).toLocaleTimeString(),
            level: logLevels[Math.floor(Math.random() * logLevels.length)],
            message: messages[Math.floor(Math.random() * messages.length)]
          }));
        };
        
        const performBackup = async () => {
          alert('å¤‡ä»½ä»»åŠ¡å·²å¯åŠ¨ï¼Œè¯·ç¨å€™...');
          // è¿™é‡Œå¯ä»¥è°ƒç”¨å®é™…çš„å¤‡ä»½ API
        };
        
        const clearCache = async () => {
          alert('ç¼“å­˜æ¸…ç†å®Œæˆï¼');
          // è¿™é‡Œå¯ä»¥è°ƒç”¨å®é™…çš„ç¼“å­˜æ¸…ç† API
        };
```

2. **ä¿®å¤åŸå§‹LocationCard.vueæ–‡ä»¶** - åˆ é™¤ç¬¬äºŒä¸ªtemplateï¼ˆç¬¬139-170è¡Œï¼‰ï¼š

```vue:/Users/huijoohwee/Documents/GitHub/299_project-test/PRJT0001_MAPSXPLR_202507201916-v0.0.1/src/components/LocationCard.vue
<template>
  <div class="location-card bg-white rounded-lg shadow-md hover:shadow-lg transition-shadow duration-200">
    <div class="p-4">
      <!-- å¡ç‰‡å¤´éƒ¨ -->
      <div class="flex justify-between items-start mb-3">
        <div class="flex-1">
          <h3 class="text-lg font-semibold text-gray-800 mb-1">{{ location.name }}</h3>
          <p class="text-sm text-gray-500">{{ formatCoordinates(location.coordinates) }}</p>
        </div>
        <div class="flex gap-1 ml-2">
          <el-button 
            @click="$emit('locate', location)"
            type="primary"
            icon="Location"
            size="small"
            circle
            title="å®šä½åˆ°æ­¤å¤„"
          />
          <el-button 
            @click="$emit('edit', location)"
            type="info"
            icon="Edit"
            size="small"
            circle
            title="ç¼–è¾‘"
          />
          <el-button 
            @click="$emit('delete', location)"
            type="danger"
            icon="Delete"
            size="small"
            circle
            title="åˆ é™¤"
          />
        </div>
      </div>
      
      <!-- æè¿° -->
      <p v-if="location.description" class="text-gray-600 text-sm mb-3">
        {{ location.description }}
      </p>
      
      <!-- æ ‡ç­¾å’Œè¯„åˆ† -->
      <div class="flex justify-between items-center">
        <div class="flex gap-2">
          <el-tag 
            v-if="location.category"
            :type="getCategoryType(location.category)"
            size="small"
          >
            {{ location.category }}
          </el-tag>
        </div>
        
        <div class="flex items-center gap-2">
          <el-rate 
            v-if="location.rating"
            v-model="location.rating"
            :disabled="!editable"
            size="small"
            @change="$emit('rate', location, $event)"
          />
          <span class="text-xs text-gray-400">{{ formatTime(location.timestamp) }}</span>
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>
  </div>
</template>

<script setup lang="ts">
import { computed } from 'vue';
import { ElButton, ElTag, ElRate } from 'element-plus';
import type { Location } from '../stores/map';

interface Props {
  location: Location;
  editable?: boolean;
}

interface Emits {
  locate: [location: Location];
  edit: [location: Location];
  delete: [location: Location];
  rate: [location: Location, rating: number];
}

const props = withDefaults(defineProps<Props>(), {
  editable: true
});

defineEmits<Emits>();

const formatCoordinates = (coords: [number, number]) => {
  return `${coords[0].toFixed(4)}, ${coords[1].toFixed(4)}`;
};

const formatTime = (timestamp: string) => {
  const date = new Date(timestamp);
  const now = new Date();
  const diff = now.getTime() - date.getTime();
  
  const minutes = Math.floor(diff / (1000 * 60));
  const hours = Math.floor(diff / (1000 * 60 * 60));
  const days = Math.floor(diff / (1000 * 60 * 60 * 24));
  
  if (minutes < 60) {
    return `${minutes}åˆ†é’Ÿå‰`;
  } else if (hours < 24) {
    return `${hours}å°æ—¶å‰`;
  } else if (days < 7) {
    return `${days}å¤©å‰`;
  } else {
    return date.toLocaleDateString('zh-CN');
  }
};

const getCategoryType = (category: string) => {
  const typeMap: Record<string, string> = {
    'é¤å…': 'success',
    'æ™¯ç‚¹': 'primary',
    'é…’åº—': 'warning',
    'è´­ç‰©': 'info',
    'äº¤é€š': 'danger'
  };
  return typeMap[category] || 'default';
};
</script>

<style scoped>
.location-card {
  @apply border border-gray-200;
}

.location-card:hover {
  @apply border-blue-300;
}
</style>
```

```css:/Users/huijoohwee/Documents/GitHub/299_project-test/PRJT0001_MAPSXPLR_202507201916-v0.0.1/src/styles/global.css
  height: 100%;
  margin: 0;

}

/* Styles for the main map container which holds the map and other UI elements */
.map-container {
  color: black;
  position: absolute;
  top: 0;
  left: 0;
  height: 100%;
  width: 100%;

  overflow: hidden;
}

  left: 0;
}

  height: 100%;
  width: 100%;
}

/* Styles for the Day Planner Mode Toggle Switch */

  display: flex;
  align-items: center;

}

  content: "";

  bottom: 3px;
  background-color: white;
  transition: .4s;
}

  background-color: #2196F3;
}

}

}

}

}

/* Styles for the timeline panel used in Day Planner mode */

}

/* Styles for the header within the timeline panel */
```
